# 💵 LA BIBLIA FINANCIERA DE FAL.AI (1312 MODELOS) — MAPA DE PRECIOS EXACTOS

> **Documento financiero maestro**: Describe los costes, precios base exactos («Pricing Info Override») y el cálculo subyacente para los todos los modelos habilitados en la plataforma.

---


# CATEGORÍA: 3D-TO-3D

## fal-ai/hunyuan-3d/v3.1/part (Hunyuan 3D Part Splitter)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.45 per generation. For $1.00, you can run this model 2 times.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Coste_Fijo_Base`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Simple)**

# CATEGORÍA: AUDIO-TO-AUDIO

## fal-ai/ace-step/audio-inpaint (ACE-Step)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.0002 per second of generated audio. For $1 you can run generate 5000 seconds (83 minutes) of music from lyrics.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**

## fal-ai/ltx-2-19b/audio-to-video (LTX-2 19B)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.0018 per megapixel of generated video data (width × height × frames), rounded up. For example, if you generate a video that is 121 frames long at 1280 × 720, your total generated video is ≈112 MP, and your request will cost $0.2016.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

---
## fal-ai/ltx-2-19b/audio-to-video/lora (LTX-2 19B)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

---
## fal-ai/flux-2-flex/edit (Flux 2 Flex)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.05** per megapixel on both input and output side, rounded up to the nearest megapixel. For example, a **1024x1024** image will cost **$0.05**, and a **1920x1080** image will cost **$0.10** (**$0.05** × **2** megapixels). Similarly, a **512x512** output will cost **$0.06** (**$0.05** for **0.26** megapixels, rounded to **1** megapixel).

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

## fal-ai/flux-2-pro/edit (Flux 2 Pro)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.03** for the first megapixel of output, plus **$0.015** per extra megapixel of input and output, rounded up to the nearest megapixel. For example, a **1024x1024** image will cost **$0.03**, and a **1920x1080** image will cost **$0.045** (**$0.03** for first megapixel + **$0.015** for the second megapixel). Similarly, a **512x512** output will cost **$0.03** (**$0.03** for**0.25** megapixels, rounded to **1** megapixel)

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

## fal-ai/gpt-image-1-mini/edit (GPT Image 1 Mini)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost different amounts based on the input and output.
- You will be charged $0.002 per 1,000 input text tokens. One word is roughly 4 tokens.
- You will be charged $0.0025 per 1,000 input image tokens. One 1024x1024 image is roughly 135 tokens.
- For **low** quality, you will be charged $0.005 for 1024x1024 or $0.006 for any other size *per output image*. 
- For **medium** quality, you will be charged $0.011 for 1024x1024 or $0.015 for any other size *per output image*.
- For **high** quality, you will be charged $0.036 for 1024x1024 or $0.052 for any other size *per output image*.
- Your total request price will be rounded up to the nearest cent.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---
## fal-ai/gpt-image-1.5/edit (GPT-Image 1.5)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost different amounts based on the number of images, quality, and size.

- You will be charged $0.005 per 1,000 input text tokens. One word is roughly 4 tokens.
- You will be charged $0.008 per 1,000 input image tokens. One 1024x1024 image is roughly 135 tokens in low fidelity mode, or 3,050 tokens in high fidelity mode.
-  You will be charged $0.010 per 1,000 output text tokens. The model will consume tokens reasoning about your prompt based on it's complexity.
- For **low** quality, you will be charged $0.009 for 1024x1024 or $0.013 for any other size *per image*. 
- For **medium** quality, you will be charged $0.034 for 1024x1024, $0.051 for 1024x1536 and $0.050 for 1536x1024 *per image*.
- For **high** quality, you will be charged $0.133 for 1024x1024, $0.200 for 1024x1536 or $0.199 for 1536x1024 *per image*.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---

- You will be charged $0.002 per 1,000 input text tokens. One word is roughly 4 tokens.
- You will be charged $0.005 per 1,000 input image tokens. One 1024x1024 image is roughly 135 tokens in low fidelity mode, or 3,050 tokens in high fidelity mode.
- For **low** quality, you will be charged $0.011 for 1024x1024 or $0.016 for any other size *per output image*. 
- For **medium** quality, you will be charged $0.042 for 1024x1024 or $0.063 for any other size *per output image*.
- For **high** quality, you will be charged $0.167 for 1024x1024 or $0.25 for any other size *per output image*.

- For **high** quality, you will be charged $0.167 for 1024x1024 or $0.25 for any other size *per output image*.

## fal-ai/nano-banana-2/edit (Nano Banana 2)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.08** per image. For **$1.00**, you can run this model **12** times. 2K and 4K outputs will be charged at **1.5** times and **2** times the standard rate, respectively. 0.5K (512px) resolution outputs will be charged at **0.75** times the standard rate. If web search is used, an additional $0.015 will be charged. If high thinking is used, an additional $0.002 will be charged. **Note: Pricing is subject to change.**

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Coste_Fijo_Base * Factor_Multiplicador_Resolucion`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Simple)**
- 🔸 **Factor de resolución (2K=1.5x, 4K=2x)**

---

## fal-ai/patina/material/extract (PATINA)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.10** plus **$0.02** per megapixel plus **$0.01** per megapixel per map type. When using 2x upscaling, an additional **$0.004** per (pre-upscaling) megapixel per map will be charged, and when using 4x upscaling, an additional **$0.016** per (pre-upscaling) megapixel per map will be charged.  For example, A 1024x1024 material with all 5 maps and no upscaling (1K) will cost **$0.17**, and a 2048x2048 material with all 5 maps and 4x upscaling (8K) will cost $0.70.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

---
## bytedance/seedance-2.0/fast/image-to-video (Seedance 2.0 Fast Image to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of 720p video you generated, you will be charged **$0.2419/second**. Your request will cost **$0.0112** per 1000 tokens. The number of tokens is given by (height of output video * width of output video * duration * 24) / 1024. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---
## bytedance/seedance-2.0/fast/reference-to-video (Seedance 2.0 Fast Reference to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of 720p video you generated, you will be charged **$0.2419/second**. Your request will cost **$0.0112** per 1000 tokens. The number of tokens is given by (height of output video * width of output video * (input video duration + output video duration) * 24) / 1024. **If video inputs are provided the price is multiplied by 0.6**. With video inputs and 720p resolution the price is **$0.14515** per second.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---
## bytedance/seedance-2.0/image-to-video (Seedance 2 Image to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of 720p video you generated, you will be charged **$0.3024/second**. Your request will cost $0.014 per 1000 tokens. The number of tokens is given by (height of output video * width of output video * duration * 24) / 1024. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---
## bytedance/seedance-2.0/reference-to-video (Seedance 2 Reference to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of 720p video you generated, you will be charged **$0.3024/second**. Your request will cost $0.014 per 1000 tokens. The number of tokens is given by (height of output video * width of output video * ( input duration + output duration) * 24) / 1024. **If video inputs are provided the price is multiplied by 0.6**. With video inputs and 720p resolution the price is **$0.1814** per second.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

## fal-ai/bytedance/seedance/v1.5/pro/image-to-video (Bytedance)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Each 720p 5 second video with audio costs roughly **$0.26**. For other resolutions, 1 million video tokens with audio costs **$2.4**. Without audio, the price is **1.2** per millition tokens. tokens(video)  = (height x width x FPS x duration) / 1024. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---

## fal-ai/kling-video/v3/pro/image-to-video (Kling Video v3 Image to Video [Pro])
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of video you generated, you will be charged **$0.112** (audio off) or **$0.168** (audio on), if voice control is used while generating audio you will be charged **$0.196**. For example, a 5s video with audio on and voice control will cost **$0.98**

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**

## fal-ai/ltx-2-19b/distilled/image-to-video (LTX-2 19B Distilled)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.0008 per megapixel of generated video data (width × height × frames), rounded up. For example, if you generate a video that is 121 frames long at 1280 × 720, your total generated video is ≈112 MP, and your request will cost $0.0896.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

---

## fal-ai/pixverse/c1/image-to-video (PixVerse C1 Image to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Billing is calculated per second of video generated. For 360p, your request will cost **$0.030** per second without audio and **$0.040** per second with audio. For 540p, it will cost **$0.040** per second without audio and **$0.050** per second with audio. For 720p, it will cost **$0.050** per second without audio and **$0.065** per second with audio. For 1080p, it will cost **$0.095** per second without audio and **$0.120** per second with audio. For **$1** you can run this model for approximately **33 seconds** at 360p (no audio) or about **10 seconds** at 1080p (no audio).

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---

> For every second of video you generate you will be charged **$0.10** without audio or **$0.15** with audio for 720p or 1080p. At 4k, you will be charged **$0.30** per second without audio, or **$0.35** with. For example, a **5 second video** at **1080p** with **audio on** will cost **$0.75**.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---

# CATEGORÍA: LLM

## fal-ai/bytedance/seed/v2/mini (Bytedance Seed 2.0 Mini)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.0001** per 1000 units. For inputs under 128k tokens, the units per input token is 1. For inputs of over 128k tokens, 2 units will be charged per token. Similarly, each output token costs 4 units, provided the total output length (reasoning + output) is under 128k tokens, and 8 units per token otherwise.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---
## fal-ai/qwen-3-guard (Qwen 3 Guard [8B])
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Precios base dinámicos bajo demanda (El modelo no tiene override público documentado).

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**

## fal-ai/flux-2-flex (Flux 2 Flex)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.05** per megapixel on both input and output side, rounded up to the nearest megapixel. For example, a **1024x1024** image will cost **$0.05**, and a **1920x1080** image will cost **$0.10** (**$0.06** × **2** megapixels). Similarly, a **512x512** output will cost **$0.05** (**$0.05** for **0.26** megapixels, rounded to **1** megapixel).

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

## fal-ai/flux-2-pro (Flux 2 Pro)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.03** for the first megapixel of output, plus **$0.015** per extra megapixel of input and output, rounded up to the nearest megapixel. For example, a **1024x1024** image will cost **$0.03**, and a **1920x1080** image will cost **$0.045** (**$0.03** for first megapixel + **$0.015** for the second megapixel). Similarly, a **512x512** output will cost **$0.03** (**$0.03** for **0.25** megapixels, rounded to **1** megapixel)

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

## fal-ai/flux-2/lora (Flux 2)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.021** per megapixel. LoRAs over 2GB in size will accrue an extra 50% charge per GB (2-3GB total lora size will multiply the price by 1.5x, 3-4GB total lora size by 2x, 4-5GB total lora size by 2.5x. The max limit is now 5GB from the older 2GB.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

## fal-ai/gpt-image-1-mini (GPT Image 1 Mini)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost different amounts based on the input and output.
- You will be charged $0.002 per 1,000 input text tokens. One word is roughly 4 tokens.
- For **low** quality, you will be charged $0.005 for 1024x1024 or $0.006 for any other size *per output image*. 
- For **medium** quality, you will be charged $0.011 for 1024x1024 or $0.015 for any other size *per output image*.
- For **high** quality, you will be charged $0.036 for 1024x1024 or $0.052 for any other size *per output image*.
- Your total request price will be rounded up to the nearest cent.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---
## fal-ai/gpt-image-1.5 (GPT-Image 1.5)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost different amounts based on the number of images, quality, and size.

- You will be charged $0.005 per 1,000 input text tokens. One word is roughly 4 tokens.
-  You will be charged $0.010 per 1,000 output text tokens. The model will consume tokens reasoning about your prompt based on it's complexity.
- For **low** quality, you will be charged $0.009 for 1024x1024 or $0.013 for any other size *per image*. 
- For **medium** quality, you will be charged $0.034 for 1024x1024, $0.051 for 1024x1536 and $0.050 for 1536x1024 *per image*.
- For **high** quality, you will be charged $0.133 for 1024x1024, $0.200 for 1024x1536 or $0.199 for 1536x1024 *per image*.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---

## fal-ai/nano-banana-2 (Nano Banana 2)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.08** per image. For **$1.00**, you can run this model **12** times. 2K and 4K outputs will be charged at **1.5** times and **2** times the standard rate, respectively. 0.5K (512px) resolution outputs will be charged at **0.75** times the standard rate. If web search is used, an additional $0.015 will be charged. If high thinking is used, an additional $0.002 will be charged. **Note: Pricing is subject to change.**

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Coste_Fijo_Base * Factor_Multiplicador_Resolucion`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Simple)**
- 🔸 **Factor de resolución (2K=1.5x, 4K=2x)**

---
## fal-ai/nano-banana-pro (Nano Banana Pro)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.15** per image. For **$1.00**, you can run this model **7** times. 4K outputs will be charged at double the standard rate. If web search is used, an additional $0.015 will be charged. Note: Pricing may change in the future.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**

## fal-ai/patina/material (PATINA)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$0.01** plus **$0.02** per megapixel plus **$0.01** per megapixel per map type. When using 2x upscaling, an additional **$0.004** per (pre-upscaling) megapixel per map will be charged, and when using 4x upscaling, an additional **$0.016** per (pre-upscaling) megapixel per map will be charged. For example, A 1024x1024 material with all 5 maps and no upscaling (1K) will cost **$0.08**, and a 2048x2048 material with all 5 maps and 4x upscaling (8K) will cost $0.61.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

## argil/avatars/text-to-video (Avatars Text to Video)

---
## bytedance/seedance-2.0/fast/text-to-video (Seedance 2.0 Fast Text to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of 720p video you generated, you will be charged **$0.2419/second**. Your request will cost **$0.0112** per 1000 tokens. The number of tokens is given by (height of output video * width of output video * duration * 24) / 1024. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---
## bytedance/seedance-2.0/text-to-video (Seedance 2.0 Text to Video API)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For every second of 720p video you generated, you will be charged **$0.3034/second**. Your request will cost $0.014 per 1000 tokens. The number of tokens is given by (height of output video * width of output video * duration * 24) / 1024. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---

---
## fal-ai/bytedance/seedance/v1.5/pro/text-to-video (Bytedance)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Each 720p 5 second video with audio costs roughly **$0.26**. For other resolutions, 1 million video tokens with audio costs **$2.4**. Without audio, the price is **1.2** per millition tokens. tokens(video)  = (height x width x FPS x duration) / 1024. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Input_Tokens * P_In) + (Output_Tokens * P_Out)`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Límite de Salida (Output Tokens) y Entrada (Input Tokens)**

---

## fal-ai/ltx-2-19b/distilled/text-to-video (LTX-2 19B Distilled)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.0008 per megapixel of generated video data (width × height × frames), rounded up. For example, if you generate a video that is 121 frames long at 1280 × 720, your total generated video is ≈112 MP, and your request will cost $0.0896.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

---

## fal-ai/magi (MAGI-1)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.80 to generate one four-second video. For $1 you can run this model approximately 1 time. 

Additional seconds will cost $0.20 each, calculated at 24 frames per second.

Additional inference steps above 16 incur a 1/16 multiplier each, such that your total cost will be multiplied x2 at 32 steps, x3 at 48 and x4 at 64. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Precio Estándar por Inferencia`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

## fal-ai/pixverse/c1/text-to-video (PixVerse C1 Text to Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Billing is calculated per second of video generated. For 360p, your request will cost **$0.030** per second without audio and **$0.040** per second with audio. For 540p, it will cost **$0.040** per second without audio and **$0.050** per second with audio. For 720p, it will cost **$0.050** per second without audio and **$0.065** per second with audio. For 1080p, it will cost **$0.095** per second without audio and **$0.120** per second with audio. For **$1** you can run this model for approximately **33 seconds** at 360p (no audio) or about **10 seconds** at 1080p (no audio).

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---

# CATEGORÍA: TRAINING

## fal-ai/ernie-image-trainer (ERNIE-Image Trainer)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost **$1.2** per **1000-step** training run. It scales per step, so a **2000-step** training run will cost **$2.4**.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Precio Estándar por Inferencia`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

---
## fal-ai/flux-2-klein-4b-base-trainer (Flux 2 Klein 4B Base Trainer)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> The cost of training depends on the number of steps. The formula is: 0.005 * steps. With 1000 steps, your request will cost **$5.00**. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Precio Estándar por Inferencia`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

---
## fal-ai/flux-2-klein-4b-base-trainer/edit (Flux 2 Klein 4B Base Trainer)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> The cost of training depends on the number of steps and the reference images. The formula is: 0.0046 * steps * reference_multiplier. The reference multiplier for 1, 2, 3 and 4 images is 2.11, 3.44, 5.09, and 6.95 respectively. With 1 reference image and 1000 steps, your request will cost **$9.71**. 

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Precio Estándar por Inferencia`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

---

## fal-ai/qwen-image-layered-trainer (Qwen Image Layered Trainer)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> The training cost depends on the number of steps and the number of layers. The formula is
**0.00425 × steps × num_of_layers**. Here, **num_of_layers** refers to the maximum number of layers per image in the dataset. For example, with 5 layers and 1,000 steps, the total cost will be **$21.25**.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Coste_Fijo_Base`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Simple)**

## clarityai/crystal-video-upscaler (Crystal Upscaler [Video])
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Pricing is **$0.10 per megapixel per second**. The total cost is multiplied based on the video’s frame rate (FPS), using **30-FPS increments**:
- Up to **30 FPS** → **1× multiplier**
- Up to **60 FPS** → **2× multiplier**
- Up to **90 FPS** → **3× multiplier**


For instance, a video upscaled to a resolution of 2440 × 1440, with a frame rate of 30 FPS and a duration of 4 seconds, is priced as follows: 
3.5 (megapixels) × 4 (seconds) × 1 (FPS multiplier for 0–30 FPS) × $0.10 = $1.40

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

---

## fal-ai/bytedance-upscaler/upscale/video (Bytedance Upscaler)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Upscaling to 1080p costs $0.0072/s, 2K costs $0.0144/s, and 4K costs $0.0288/s, at a 30fps rate. Processing at 60fps doubles the cost for any resolution. Processing in `pro` mode makes the price 10 times of the normal price ($0.072/s, $0.144/s, $0.288/s for 1080p,2K, 4K at 30fps respectively, at 60fps these prices are further doubled.)

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Coste_Fijo_Base * Factor_Multiplicador_Resolucion`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Simple)**
- 🔸 **Factor de resolución (2K=1.5x, 4K=2x)**

## fal-ai/kling-video/o3/pro/video-to-video/edit (Kling O3 Edit Video [Pro])
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**

## fal-ai/ltx-2-19b/distilled/extend-video (LTX-2 19B Distilled)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.0008 per megapixel of context frames plus generated video data (width × height × frames), rounded up. For example, if you generate a video that is 121 frames long at 1280 × 720, your total generated video is ≈112 MP, and your request will cost $0.0896.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Resolución geométrica (Ancho x Alto)**

---

## fal-ai/magi-distilled/extend-video (MAGI-1 (Distilled))
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Your request will cost $0.32 to generate one four-second video. For $1 you can run this model approximately 3 times. 

Additional seconds will cost $0.08 each, calculated at 24 frames per second.

Additional inference steps above 16 incur a 1/16 multiplier each, such that your total cost will be multiplied x2 at 32 steps.

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Coste_Fijo_Base`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Simple)**

## fal-ai/pixverse/v6/extend (Pixverse)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Billing is calculated per second of video generated. For 360p, your request will cost **$0.025** per second without audio and **$0.035** per second with audio. For 540p, it will cost **$0.035** per second without audio and **$0.045** per second with audio. For 720p, it will cost **$0.045** per second without audio and **$0.060** per second with audio. For 1080p, it will cost **$0.090** per second without audio and **$0.115** per second with audio. For **$1** you can run this model for approximately **40 seconds** at 360p (no audio) or about **11 seconds** at 1080p (no audio).

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

`Coste = (Ancho * Alto / 1,000,000) * Precio_Base_MP`

`Coste = Precio Estándar por Inferencia`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

---
## fal-ai/wan/v2.2-14b/animate/move (Wan-2.2 Animate Move)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> Request is billed based on the number of frames, at a rate of **16 frames per "video second"**:

- **720p:** $0.08 per video second
- **580p:** $0.06 per video second
- **480p:** $0.04 per video second

**How to calculate your cost:**

1. Total frames = video duration × fps
2. Video seconds (billed) = total frames ÷ 16
3. Cost = video seconds × price per second

**Example — 5-second video at 60 fps, 720p:**
- Total frames = 5 × 60 = 300 frames
- Video seconds (billed) = 300 ÷ 16 = 18.75
- Cost = 18.75 × $0.08 = **$1.50**

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Precio Estándar por Inferencia`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Petición Determinista (Generación Fija)**

---

## xai/grok-imagine-video/edit-video (Grok Imagine Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For a 6s 480p video your request will cost **$0.36** (**$0.05** per second of video output + **$0.01** per second of video input). At an output resolution of 480p, every second costs **$0.06** (**$0.05** for output and **$0.01** for input), and at 720p, every second costs **$0.08** (**$0.07** for output and **$0.01** for input)

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**

---
## xai/grok-imagine-video/extend-video (Grok Imagine Extend Video)
**💰 Coste Base Fal.ai:**
> For a 6s 480p video your request will cost **$0.36** (**$0.05** per second of video output + **$0.01** per second of video input). At an output resolution of 480p, every second costs **$0.06** (**$0.05** for output and **$0.01** for input), and at 720p, every second costs **$0.08** (**$0.07** for output and **$0.01** for input)

**📐 Fórmula Matemática Implicada:**
`Coste = Segundos * Precio_Base_Seg_Video * Factor_Resol_Calidad`

**⚙️ Variables de Coste Impactadas:**
- 🔸 **Duración temporal (Segundos)**
- 🔸 **Escalado por Resolución (Ej: 720p vs 1080p)**
